Japanese Disrupt Financial Plans 61

Using News Agencies to Create an Unstable Atmosphere

Buying Cash in Wuhan Reaches 5 Million Yuan

Wuhan Communication: After the Japanese forcibly occupied the three northeastern provinces by force, they tried their best to destroy the internal security. At the same time, they also tried their best to disrupt the finances of various commercial ports. Military and economic aggression has really been carried out in two ways. All the chaotic situations such as the decline of public bonds and the exhaustion of finance are caused by the Japanese sabotage. Recently, Nanjing and Hankou have discovered this plan of the Japanese. The details obtained in Hankou are especially detailed. First, the Japanese in Hankou used good merchants and unscrupulous people to send telegrams to Beijing and Shanghai, creating various rumors to make the ports influence each other and create economic panic. The general agency for creating rumors is the Daily News and the United News Agency run by the Japanese. For example, the recent publication that only a dozen Qianzhuan businesses can operate in Hankou, and Shanghai banks are also in danger, and the Qianye Association requested the government to stop the anti-Japanese movement, etc., are all deliberately making alarming remarks and confusing the audience. After the Qianye Association, the Bank Association, and the General Chamber of Commerce petitioned the government to protest, they automatically made corrections, but the financial situation in Hankou has been slightly affected. On the 6th of this month, the newspaper published another news that "Qianzhuan businesses in Hankou went bankrupt again", saying that two Qianzhuan businesses in Hankou went bankrupt again. In fact, the two Qianzhuan businesses that suspended business recently, Huitong and Heng'an, were temporarily suspending business to clear accounts, not bankruptcy. The intention of creating this atmosphere again and again is beyond question. Unexpectedly, on the 7th, according to a certain source, the Japanese financial destruction plan is not limited to this. The most poisonous one is to buy a large amount of cash, which is carried out simultaneously in Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, Hankou, Guangzhou, Hong Kong, and Jinan. It is planned to buy 5 million yuan every day, and a total of 450 million yuan will be bought within three months. It is heard that the effect of buying in Beijing and Shanghai is less, while Hankou has achieved the first step of success. In the past ten days, the amount of the purchase has reached 5 million yuan. To this day, it is still buying about 500,000 yuan every day. The managers are the Hankou Banks of Zhengjin, Mitsubishi, and Mitsui. There are also some Chinese traitors who are used by them. This is indeed a serious problem that cannot be ignored (December 7).

Part of Japan's Illegal Pending Cases (II) 62

The Japanese Warship Destroying Chinese Ships and Killing Chinese People Near Magai, Miaojie Case: In June of the 9th year of the Republic of China, a Chai Feng ship dispatched by the Chinese fleet was near Magai, Russia. When it encountered the Japanese fleet, the ship immediately dropped anchor and moored and raised two national flags to avoid misunderstandings. However, the Japanese warship fired artillery, about eight or nine shots in total, sinking it, resulting in the injury and death of 34 boatmen and laborers. Afterwards, the ship was burned. Moreover, the Chinese captain and the Chinese consul stationed in Miaojie had repeatedly asked Japanese military officers to pay attention to the Chinese firewood transport ship near Magai. The military officers also agreed. On December 31 of the 9th year, our side sent a note to the Japanese ambassador based on the above facts, proposing four solutions: (1) The Japanese government should apologize to the Chinese government for the entire case. (2) The Japanese warship officers and soldiers who bombed the Chinese Feng ship should be investigated and severely punished, and the handling should be notified to China. (3) The 34 dead laborers and one seriously injured person should be given compensation. (4) The destroyed ship and all items in the ship should be compensated according to the number. The Japanese side said that the ship not only ignored the Japanese warship's request to moor, but also tried to escape, so it was shelled. Because it was feared that the ship would be used by the enemy, it was burned. The measures taken by the Japanese warship are in line with Article 63 of the London Declaration of 1909 and Article 49, and Articles 95, 96, 126, and 141 of the Japanese Naval Warfare Regulations. The Japanese government cannot bear the responsibility of compensation and other responsibilities, etc. On February 15 of the 11th year, the former Ministry of Foreign Affairs based on the naval ministry's review that the Feng ship had no resistance ability and no resistance behavior at that time. According to the London Declaration and Japanese Naval Warfare Regulations, the Japanese army did not confiscate the Feng ship. Moreover, it was hastily shelled. Also, the Japanese army's handling at that time was completely contrary to Article 49 of the London Declaration and Article 126 of the Japanese Naval Warfare Regulations, which said that destruction and proper inspection should not be done. The regulations cannot be applied at all, etc., rebutting the Japanese ambassador and requesting that the four articles of the premise be followed up and agreed as soon as possible. After that, they were repeatedly urged, but there were no results.

Jilin Hunchun Case: On October 2 of the 9th year of the Republic of China, bandits attacked Gong Hunchun and burned the Japanese consulate. 21 Japanese and Korean people died and 19 were injured. Japan immediately sent four squadrons and six detachments of troops to enter the country one after another. The Japanese ambassador put forward four requirements: (1) condolences, (2) compensation, (3) punishing those responsible, and (4) apology. In April of the 11th year, the Japanese ambassador submitted a list of losses, requesting that they be dealt with as soon as possible along with other items. Our side discussed with the Japanese ambassador that the Japanese army had entered the country without authorization and infringed on our sovereignty, and that the apology should be made by both sides. It was difficult to deal with the officials and according to the report of the Yanji Daoyin, in July of the 11th year, the losses suffered by the Chinese people and reclamation people in the five counties of Yanbian due to the entry of the Japanese army were proposed, and the Japanese side was asked to compensate. The pension and medical expenses of 24 Chinese people who died, 4 seriously injured, and 314 reclamation people were declared reserved. According to the Japanese ambassador's proposal, the two sides first sent personnel to exchange opinions. The Japanese side put forward the items of condolences for the Japanese and Korean people and property losses, totaling more than 464,000 Japanese yen. Our side based on the report of Yanji Daoyin, 242,000 yuan for property losses of Chinese people, more than 1 million yuan for reclamation people, and 459,000 yuan for pensions for Chinese people, and 1.986 million yuan for pensions for reclamation people. The commissioners of both parties negotiated repeatedly. The Japanese side said that Korean people cannot leave the country, and reclamation people are Japanese, and Japan cannot compensate them. As for the request for the Japanese government to apologize, the Japanese side said that the Japanese army dispatched troops based on the right of self-defense under international law and insisted on withdrawing the counterclaim. Our side rebutted and expressed that if the Japanese side could agree to apologize, the reclamation people's request could be discussed and concessions could be made. The Japanese side still insisted on not agreeing, and the contact was suspended. After that, they were repeatedly urged, and the Japanese ambassador has not yet given a specific answer.

Case of Japanese Man Xiaomiao Mitaku Assisting Bandits to Disrupt the Border: On September 24 of the 11th year, Jilin troops suppressed bandits and found that there was a Japanese man in the Idiot Team. They seized the Japanese man Xiaomiao near Yu Jiabao, and he carried official posts and silver ornaments. He confessed that he first worked as a coolie, and then joined the Idiot Team with the Japanese man Endo who had joined the Idiot Team earlier to fight bandits, intending to help the most Chinese bandits to disrupt the border in order to prepare for diplomatic excuses for his country to seize power. The bandits' weapons were not sold by them, but were supplied by their country. All the two machine guns were transported from their country to Toutaogou, Jiandao, nominally robbed by bandits, but actually delivered. The money, silver ornaments, etc., were stolen goods divided from successive robberies, etc. The Jilin Special Envoy transferred the person to the Japanese Consulate in Jilin for disposal and protested. On November 18, our side notified the Japanese ambassador, and told him that the world had long rumored that the Japanese military intelligence agencies secretly assisted bandits to disrupt our border in order to achieve their purpose of advancing troops to station police. Judging from the discovery of munitions in Harbin and the personal confession of the Japanese man Xiaotoku this time, it is indeed an undeniable fact that the Japanese have been helping Chinese bandits along the border. Please convey to your government to severely punish and strictly prohibit it. According to the reply, the Japanese man had no assistance to the bandits. The previous confession was forced by Battalion Commander Li. We immediately rebutted the Japanese ambassador based on the facts, and still asked him to handle it in accordance with our previous note. On December 14 of the 20th year, they were urged again, but there was no reply.

Transfer of Qingdao Observatory (formerly known as Qingdao Meteorological Observatory) Japanese Personnel Case: When Qingdao was taken over in the 11th year of the Republic of China, the Japanese refused to return the Qingdao Meteorological Observatory on the grounds that our country did not have meteorological professionals for a while. After the Shandong Case Rehabilitation Governor and the Japanese ambassador negotiated repeatedly, eight measures were formulated, including allowing our country to send personnel to the office to jointly handle the matter, and Japanese personnel would continue to serve temporarily. The former Beijing Ministry of Foreign Affairs repeatedly negotiated with the Japanese side. The Japanese ambassador had an expression of starting negotiations, but there was no result. In August of the 18th year, our side, according to Article 5 (3) of the Annex to the Shandong Pending Case Details Agreement, "When Chinese Meteorological Observatory staff are trained in the future, and the old staff is transferred, the method of reporting and contacting the Japanese Meteorological Observatory will be changed" and sent personnel to negotiate with the Japanese side. Our side proposed seven measures to determine the method of reporting and contacting the Japanese Meteorological Observatory after the Japanese personnel of the Qingdao Observatory were transferred. The Japanese side also proposed seven measures and three items for understanding. The sections in which the observation and investigation of geomagnetism and gas at the Qingdao Observatory were to be presided over by Japanese technicians were in conflict with the above provisions. After repeated negotiations, it was not resolved. In January of the 19th year, our side continued to urge the Japanese side to consult as soon as possible. He replied that the Chinese staff had been replaced a lot, and the technology had not been degraded, and the instruments used were French style, which was inconvenient for the Japanese meteorological report and contact. He also said that both China and Japan had geomagnetism observations at the Qingdao Observatory, and the Japanese side asked to study and compare with each other, but the Chinese side did not agree and directly sent the observations to the Dutch Bilt Meteorological Publication. It is observed that the publication of the station is not accurate, which is particularly relevant to the navigation of Japanese ships in Qingdao. All of the above were rebutted one by one and requested that technicians be sent as soon as possible to consult with our side on the method of reporting and contacting after the transfer. After that, they repeatedly urged the Japanese ambassador but there was no reply.

Abolishing the South Manchurian Japanese Post Case: At the Washington Conference, our country proposed to abolish the foreign posts in China. At that time, the Japanese representative had presented his opinion on the Japanese posts in the South Manchurian Railway area at the conference table. After repeated discussions, it was recognized that Japan only had transit rights in the South Manchurian Railway area, and the Japanese representative had no different words. After the General Assembly decided, all post offices in China from England, the United States, France, Japan and other countries, except for leased areas and treaty permits, were abolished before January 1, 1923. In July of the 11th year of the Republic of China (1922), the Japanese ambassador proposed to send personnel to discuss various agreements after the abolition of Japanese posts. In August, the committee of both parties met in Beijing. In addition to signing various new postal agreements, an attached document stated that the Japanese post issue in the South Manchurian Railway area would be further negotiated by the governments of the two countries in the future. After that, the Japanese ambassador was repeatedly notified and the abolition proposal was repeated, but there was no result. According to the Postal Administration's report in May of the 17th year, the number of Japanese post offices and post offices in the South Manchurian Railway area had reached more than 60.

Changsha June 1 Case: On June 1 of the 12th year of the Republic of China, when the Nisshin Company merchant ship Wuling Maru arrived in Changsha, it happened that the citizens were giving speeches on the river bank, and the crowd gathered to watch, obstructing the landing of passengers. The Japanese warship Fushimi suddenly dispatched unarmed sailors to land to show off its power. After the Hunan provincial government tried its best to suppress and requested the Japanese consul to protect and request a withdrawal, it was invalid. The warship then dispatched 20 armed soldiers to land when the crowd gradually dispersed. Under the command of an officer, they suddenly fired at the crowd, killing two unarmed citizens and seriously injuring 15 people. The deaths and injuries were all outside the Japanese merchant wharf, which showed that the pursuit at that time was not an act of self-defense. After the case occurred, the former Ministry of Foreign Affairs protested to the Japanese ambassador on the 5th based on the Hunan provincial report on June 3. On the 6th, it notified the Japanese ambassador based on the articles proposed by Hunan Province. The original conditions were as follows: (1) The commander and soldiers who shot and killed the Chinese people this time must be severely punished in accordance with Japanese military law and the handling must be notified to the Chinese officials. (2) The Chinese people who were shot and injured must be given generous pensions. (3) The commander of the Japanese fleet must apologize to the Hunan provincial officials. (4) The Japanese government must also express its apology to the Chinese government in an official document. (5) The Japanese government guarantees that such incidents will not happen again in the future. At the same time, it telegraphed Ambassador Wang stationed in Japan to negotiate with the Japanese government, and the ministry sent a commissioner to Hunan to investigate. It repeatedly urged the Japanese ambassador and the Japanese government to agree to the five items proposed. The Japanese government insisted that the sailors' actions were legitimate defense. After official correspondence, the two parties met and negotiated, but the case has not been closed. On June 4 of the 20th year, our side requested the Japanese representative to telegraph the Japanese government in accordance with the above five articles, and they were quickly dealt with, but there was still no definite reply (to be continued).

Planned Works for the Sea Walls of Jiangsu Province 63

Urgent Projects to be Undertaken First

Funding Has Been Secured

The sea walls along the southern Jiangsu province have suffered from neglect in recent years due to insufficient funding and the cessation of annual repairs. Damage to the walls is widespread, with most of the gentle slopes collapsing and the pilings resembling broken teeth. Even some of the new cement structures are showing signs of damage and shifting. In the event of a breach, the old Suzhou, Songjiang, and Taicang regions would be devastated. Shen Baozhang, the acting director of the former Jiangnan Sea Wall Office, under the instruction of the Construction Department, has conducted a thorough assessment of the post-disaster reconstruction efforts in each county. He has already drafted a plan with charts, estimating a total cost of 1,302,914 silver dollars for labor and materials. The most critical projects, which require immediate attention, include the Xuejiatan and Zhangjiazai areas in Baoshan, the military review platform in Taicang, the Xuliujingkou area in Changshu, and the third phase of supplementary works in Songjiang. However, the total cost is substantial. Given the aftermath of the disaster and the depleted state of the treasury, raising the necessary funds may prove difficult. The current Construction Department Director, Shen Baixian, believes that the sea wall project is crucial to the lives and livelihoods of the people, and that every effort must be made despite the financial difficulties. It is reported that he intends to prioritize projects based on their urgency and the current economic capacity, ensuring that the most critical areas are addressed without delay, while the less urgent projects can be completed in sequence. The cost of these urgent projects is estimated at 362,363 silver dollars, which will be offset by 300,000 silver dollars from the provincial capital construction fund within the construction bonds and 300,000 silver dollars from the Zhenjiang port improvement project. It is reported that the Provincial Government Committee has already resolved to proceed accordingly.

Songjiang 64

Hu Yinglong Sentenced to Fifteen Years: The case of Hu Yinglong, who was initially acquitted of murdering his wife, has been reviewed after the prosecutor appealed. Wuxi 65

Major Fire Outside the South Gate: The Tongshouchun Pharmacy outside the South Gate, near Huangni Bridge, caught fire yesterday (the 9th) at approximately 2:00 AM. An electrical short in the lighting wires went unnoticed while everyone was asleep, allowing the fire to spread to the building. Flames quickly erupted through the roof. By the time the local fire brigade arrived to extinguish the fire, it had already spread to the adjacent Tonghe Silk Fabric Shop. Shortly after, it spread to the opposite Rongchangxiang Foreign Goods Store, Fuxian Tea House, Liu Yonggen Barber Shop, and four other businesses including a large pancake shop. Despite the efforts of multiple fire brigades, the fire could not be contained. It was finally extinguished after 5:00 AM. In total, four buildings housing Tongshouchun and Tonghe were completely destroyed, and parts of the Rongchangxiang and Fuxian Tea House buildings were also destroyed. The Yuanchang Silk Fabric Shop, Tianxiang Silver Shop, and Chawanting Foreign Goods Store were also affected, with damage to their roofs. The total losses are estimated to be substantial. The wife of Wang Zhonghe, the owner of Tongshouchun, jumped from the upper floor and fractured her leg. She is currently receiving treatment in a hospital.

Large Numbers of Refugees Expelled: On the 6th, at 5:00 PM, over five hundred boats arrived at Xishiqiao and Lubugang in the Sixth District, carrying over two thousand male and female famine refugees from Yancheng. Verification of Disaster Victims: Jiaxing suffered from severe flooding, and the county requested disaster relief funds from the charity association. The Zhejiang Provincial Disaster Relief Association instructed the county to accurately investigate the number of affected households to facilitate relief efforts. The county government divided the area into districts and sent officials to verify the number of affected households. This process has now been completed. A total of 2,385 households, comprising 9,530 people, have been identified as disaster victims. A list of affected households has been kept in the county for use by relief workers when they arrive to distribute aid.

Gamblers Arrested and Escape in Xincheng: Gambling is rampant in Xincheng. The police officers returned to the bureau to report the incident. Shaoxing 70

Citizens Refuse to Swear Oath of Registration: In Shaoxing, many citizens with qualifications to vote refuse to swear the oath during registration. The County reported to the provincial government to request instructions. Yesterday it has been instructed by the Civil Affairs Department, stating that the county magistrates and district chiefs are responsible for the training of the public, and should find ways to arouse the political interest and responsibility of those who are qualified to vote but refuse to swear the oath, instead of let them give up. Those who have not sworn the oath, even if they have the qualifications to vote and to be candidates, as they are not included in the list of citizens, shall not be included in the list of candidates, and shall not have the right to vote and be elected in the towns.

Xiaoshan 71

Lida Paper Mill Scheduled to Open: Xiaoshan is known for its agricultural products: silkworms in the east, tobacco leaves in the west, and bamboo paper in the south. The paper mill in the south, initiated by County Magistrate Lin, has now been reorganized as a joint public-private enterprise. The county government approved the establishment of the Lida Paper Mill. Preparations are underway, and a special agent was sent to Wuxi yesterday to purchase machinery. The mill is scheduled to open once the machinery arrives.

District Chiefs Hold Joint Meeting After Town Mayor is Kidnapped: The town and village chiefs of the First District of Xiaoshan held their first joint meeting on the 7th at Jiang Temple in the urban area. Over thirty people are attending including the town and village chief Yang Peijun. Four resolutions were made: (1) 25% of the autonomous household donations collected will go to the district, with the remainder going to the towns and villages to cover expenses. (2) The expenses of the security corps leaders will be allocated by the 36 towns and villages based on the district standard of 40 yuan per leader (6 leaders). (3) An autonomous personnel research association will be established to research at any time. (4) Autonomous personnel must not go beyond their scope and should self-report to uphold autonomy.

Special Report on Educational News

A Little Advice on Elementary School Students' Patriotic Speech Competition 72

Qin

The Shanghai Education Community United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association hosted an elementary school student speech contest on the 5th of this month at Wuben Girls' School in Nanshi. Twenty-nine elementary schools attended the event. The students were full of spirit and spoke fluently and freely, and it is worth noting that the top five students were all girls. In terms of the meaning of the speeches, they were generally very good, and can be summarized into the following categories:

(1) Boycotting Japanese goods and refusing to cooperate with the Japanese at any time or place, implementing economic severance.

(2) Strengthening the body and cultivating the spirit of enduring hardship.

(3) Striving for learning; wanting to defeat a strong enemy requires first knowing yourself and knowing your enemy. In this era of scientific advancement, it is especially necessary to study science to revitalize the country. (4) Saving money for national salvation; saving the money spent on candy to accumulate a larger sum for national salvation.

The above four methods are all appropriate. When we talk about saving the country, it should be regarded as an inviolable principle. If we can expand upon these ideas and implement them throughout the country, not only will the teachers and students in schools be engaged in researching methods to save the country and cultivate a patriotic spirit to work hard to save the country, but also the families of the students will inevitably be slightly influenced.

However, in addition to the above-mentioned benefits, I have a little advice regarding this speech competition. The meaning and drafting of the speeches can be done in cooperation between teachers and students. For example, after teachers and students jointly discuss and research the meaning of the speeches, the students should draft the speeches themselves, and then the teachers should revise them. In this way, the effect of working together can be achieved in terms of work, and children can be given more opportunities to be automatic in terms of teaching.

However, most of the speeches of the children this time were in the tone of adults. From this point of view, I am afraid that the original speeches were mostly done by the teachers. If that is the case, then the students' speeches cannot avoid the drawback of being like a record player. I sincerely hope that patriotic comrades in the academic community will research and improve this aspect, and I hope to work hard to implement the above four methods.

Important News

[P Report on Educational Innovation Work of the Ministry of Education (I)

November of the 20th Year

The Ministry of Education recently submitted a report on its innovation work in November of the 20th year to the Executive Yuan for record. The original text of the report is as follows:

(I) Higher Education

(1) Matters relating to universities and colleges

An order was issued to the national colleges to exempt students from the provinces of Hubei, Jiangxi, Hunan, Anhui, Henan and the Jiangbei districts of Jiangsu Province from tuition and miscellaneous fees this year. An order was also issued to the provincial and municipal education departments to instruct all public and registered private colleges to reduce or exempt tuition fees for students from the above-mentioned disaster areas. An order was issued to the national colleges to exempt students from the provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Suiyuan, and Chahar from tuition and miscellaneous fees. An order was also issued to the provincial and municipal education departments to instruct all public and registered private colleges to reduce or exempt tuition fees for students from the above-mentioned disaster areas. The board of directors of the Beijing Private Sino-French University was approved to establish and register the school. Supervisor Xiang Jutantan was sent to inspect the Nanjing Private Cultural College. Supervisor Wang Shenming was sent to inspect the Jinan Private Qilu University, the Beijing Private Sino-French University, the Beijing Private People's College, and the Taiyuan Private Bingzhou College. Supervisor Xiang Yukai was sent to inspect the Wuchang Private Huazhong University of Wuchang and the Changsha Private Xiangya Medical College. Supervisor Lin Ben was sent to inspect the Shanghai Private Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts.

(2) Matters relating to studying abroad

Approval was granted for the issuance of public-funded study abroad certificates to a total of five people: two to the United Kingdom, two to the United States, and one to Germany. Approval was granted for the issuance of self-funded study abroad certificates to a total of twelve people: one to the United Kingdom, one to the United States, one to Germany, four to France, four to Belgium, and one to India.

(II) Secondary Education

(1) A list of private secondary schools approved for record in November: Beichu Junior High School, Xiangyang, Hubei; Gaoyang Junior Vocational School, Gaoyang, Hebei; Meng Women's Middle School, Wuxian, Jiangsu. (2) The board of directors of private secondary schools approved for record in November: Yingnian Junior High School Board of Directors, Pengxian, Sichuan. (3) The "Principles of Vocational Education Facilities" was translated and sent to League of Nations educational experts for reference. (4) Six questions about secondary normal and vocational schools were raised and sent to League of Nations educational experts for research.

(III) Elementary Education

(1) Answers to the questions about elementary schools from League of Nations Educational Expert Donner. (2) Two questions about elementary schools were raised and sent to League of Nations educational experts for research.

(IV) Overseas Chinese Education

(1) A list of overseas Chinese schools approved for record in November: Mingde Elementary School, Singapore; Peizhi Elementary School; Singapore Chunghwa Weixin Elementary School, same as above; Minnan Elementary School, North Borneo; Pei Ying Elementary School, same as above; Nanyang Rendan Elementary School, Penang; Xinhua Elementary School, same as above; Maloju Chunghwa Elementary School, Makassar. (2) An order was issued to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education and the Guangdong and Fujian Provincial Departments of Education to establish schools in conjunction with the Party, requiring Chinese businessmen going abroad to be proficient in the language of the country they are going to before being allowed to travel.

(V) Matters relating to general education

(1) Discussed the reform of Chinese education with the League of Nations educational expert delegation. (2) An order was issued to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to require all levels of schools under their jurisdiction to add several hours of lectures each week on the history of Japanese imperialism's aggression.

(VI) Social Education

(1) In conjunction with the Ministry of Interior, a submission was made to the Executive Yuan through the Antiquities Preservation Committee, requesting the revision of the Antiquities Preservation Law and its implementing regulations. Opinions were presented on the formulation and implementation of measures for the preservation and retrieval of lost items, and a request was made to promulgate the organizational regulations of the Central Antiquities Management Committee for review and compliance. (2) In conjunction with the Ministry of Interior, the 21st year Han Chinese Civil Calendar and the Han Chinese Tibetan Civil Calendar were promulgated. (3) A consultation was sent to the Ministry of Interior in response to the consultation regarding the revision of the Film Censorship Law and its implementing regulations, requesting that they be examined. (4) An urgent telegram was sent to the education departments of the nine provinces of Fujian, Shaanxi, Yunnan, Hunan, Guizhou, Guangdong, Sichuan, Gansu, and Qinghai, urging them to fill out and submit the statistical table of the general situation of social education in the 18th year within one week of receiving the document for compilation. (5) In conjunction with the Ministry of Interior, a submission was made to the Executive Yuan in response to the review and approval of the contract between the Palace Museum and engineer Yang Xinde for the joint establishment of a printing house, requesting approval. (6) An order was issued to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to distribute the general situation of social education in the country in the 17th year. (7) An order was issued to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to fill in the national language regional situation survey form, which was to be imprinted and abolished, and to send it directly to the National Language Unification Preparatory Committee. (8) An order was issued to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to issue a comparison of the literacy movement publicity held in the three provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Nanjing for reference, and to report the recent developments and specific plans for evaluation. (9) An urgent telegram was sent to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to print and distribute the 20th year social education funding table, ordering them to fill it in within the time limit. (10) An order was issued to the education departments of all provinces and municipalities to collect children's toys related to the Three Principles of the People, and to earnestly handle the matter according to the order.

National Government Responds to Students of Universities and Middle Schools 73

The Secretariat of the National Government telegraphed the Shanghai University and Middle School Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association on the 8th, stating: "To be immediately forwarded to the Shanghai Mayor Zhang, to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of University and Middle School Students: We have received the message from the Chairman. The government's established policy towards Japan remains unchanged. We are determined to defend ourselves and will never lose an inch of territory. At the same time, we appeal to the international community, gather the power of justice, and use sanctions against the violent. The so-called establishment of a neutral zone in Jinzhou, the so-called direct Sino-Japanese negotiations, are not only not advocated, but have been announced in detail and published in newspapers. The people of the country should all see this. Why the doubt? In the League of Nations case, the Japanese have been cunning and deceitful, creating new complications and making unreasonable demands. Representative Shi has been strictly protesting for days and will never make concessions that harm the country. This Chairman has long been determined to sacrifice himself for the country. As long as the people do not disrupt their steps, we will surely do our best to defend the country. All the worries of the students are being considered by the government. However, the appointment of personnel and administration are within the government's authority. In this time of national crisis, should there be discordant opinions, much suspicion and obstruction. Regarding diplomacy, the people should only observe the facts and plan for its success. This is what all true patriots should understand. As for the request to release the students of Peking University and Central University, no student in the Central Government has lost his freedom. The Peking University demonstration group, however, after arriving in Beijing, publicly announced demonstrations, refused reception of leaflets and slogans, and openly expressed agitation, disruption and overthrow of the government. The military police dissuaded them, but they acted violently. For the sake of order, it was necessary to transfer some of them to another place for isolation and supervision. They have now been sent back to Peiping. There is no so-called release. The government loves and protects the youth and will never allow the youth and reactionaries to achieve their sacrifices. The poisonous schemes of the youth have been tolerated in many ways, and the facts are there. The students need not lightly believe rumors and hastily apply. In summary, this telegram not only misunderstands the true meaning of democracy and the responsibilities of the people, but also sets a deadline for a reply, treating the government as a hostile country. Such unprecedented demands are truly appalling. Even if it is said that words are chosen in haste, should they not be self-examined to this point? Considering that the government treats the youth and students as teachers treat their children, we still uphold the duty of teaching and make a detailed announcement. The association is a collection of university students, who are committed to saving the country and know the country's crisis. They must take responsibility as patriotic youth, distinguish between safety and danger, trust the government, abide by discipline, and not be taken advantage of by reactionaries to aggravate the foreign troubles of the enemy. This is of utmost importance. This is a special decree from the Secretariat of the National Government."

Moreover, the government has repeatedly sought to be in unison with the people. If the government's attitude is first hesitant and uncertain, how can it be held accountable to the people? Mrs. Moody Returns to Shanghai This Morning 86

Tomorrow's Return to America Match Canceled

Defeated by Fincher in Hong Kong Performance

Tennis Queen Mrs. Moody will return here from Hong Kong with her husband on the President Coolidge this morning, and will leave Shanghai for America tomorrow morning.

Shanghai's Good Fortune is Too Shallow, Performance Canceled

Mrs. Moody has decided to take the original ship and leave Shanghai for America tomorrow morning, only staying here for twenty-four hours. The Lawn Tennis Association sent a telegram to the ship yesterday, but did not receive a reply late at night. Therefore, they had no choice but to announce the cancellation of the performance match. Those who have reserved seats can go to the Shishi Yanghang tomorrow to retrieve the reservation fee. Mrs. Moody gave one performance in Hong Kong, with one win and one loss.

Lost One Singles Match to Fincher

On the afternoon of the eighth, in light rain and a gentle breeze, everyone took the stage to perform until the end, and the rain still did not stop. The opponent for Mrs. Moody's singles match was Fincher, a famous Hong Kong player who had represented the inter-port team. Although the weather was bad, the audience was large. Only one set was played, with the score at 5-5, 6-6, and then 7-7. The atmosphere suddenly became tense. Continuing, they tied at 9-9. At this point, Mrs. Moody showed impatience and then lost two consecutive games, losing 11-9. Fincher's victory required great effort.

Adding Flowers to the Brocade, a Great Victory in Doubles

She then paired with HD Lunqiang to perform doubles against Luo Wenhuan and SA Lunqiang. As a result, she was like a tiger with wings, invincible. Adding flowers to the brocade, she showed her beauty even more. Swinging left and hitting right, coordinating well, Mrs. Moody and Lunqiang won a great victory with a score of 6-2, 7-5. The audience was amazed.

Talks with American, British, and Japanese Tennis Players

Someone went to ask Mrs. Moody, and the conversation touched on tennis players from various countries. Mrs. Moody said that Japanese women's tennis is still in its infancy, but they are eager to learn and have great hopes. (What about our country?) This year's British tennis is a glorious era of revival. Defeating America in the Davis Cup, Austin, the number one player, is enough to compete with anyone in the world. The same is true for Bailey. Women players are emerging like a rising wind and surging clouds, with boundless hope and a bright future. As for America's Vines, he is a teenage genius who defeated all American players and the British Bailey this year to rank first, looking down on the world with ease.

Local News

University Students Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 91

When the Anti-Japanese Associations of Various Universities Met Yesterday

Xu Xiucen, Representative of Peking University, Was Suddenly Kidnapped

Jiang Xueqian, Representative of Central University, Was Beaten and Injured

Mayor Zhang Promised to Investigate and Hold Responsible Personnel Accountable

Petitioning Students Had Not Dispersed as of 3:00 AM This Morning

Xu Xiucen, representative of the Peking University delegation to petition in Beijing, and Jiang Xueqian, representative of Central University, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday to report to all sectors and request assistance. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Shanghai United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Various Universities held its 21st Representative Conference at the Ximen Juvenile Propaganda Group. Representatives from various schools attended, and Xu and Jiang were also invited to attend. During the meeting, more than ten people in plain clothes were eavesdropping. After the meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM, there were also more than ten plainclothes people outside the door who kidnapped Xu Xiucen, the representative of Peking University, into a car and sped away. Jiang Xueqian, the representative of Central University, was severely beaten and injured. More than 5,000 students petitioned the Municipal Government at 4:00 PM, forming an encirclement. Mayor Zhang immediately agreed to suspend Chen Xizeng, Director of the Public Security Bureau, from his duties for investigation and to arrest and apprehend Tao Baichuan, a member of the Municipal Party Committee. The students demanded that they would not leave the Municipal Government until the arrested students were released. As of this newspaper's press time this morning, they had not yet dispersed. Yesterday afternoon at 5:50 PM, the Municipal Party Headquarters was also vandalized and its equipment destroyed. Martial law was declared in the French Concession in the evening. The detailed account of the incident is summarized below:

Attending the Meeting Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the 21st Representative Conference of the United Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Various Universities was held inside the Xiaoximen Juvenile Propaganda Group. Representatives from 29 universities attended, chaired by Wen Guangyi of Jinan University and recorded by Zhu Zushun of Fudan University. Various cases were discussed. During the meeting, Xu Xiucen, the representative of the Peking University delegation to Shanghai, gave a passionate speech, mentioning several points: (1) The Peking University delegation was detained in Xiaolingwei, suffering from hunger and cold. (2) The delegation was bound with ropes by police and soldiers and taken to a car in heavy rain at 3:00 AM in the middle of the night and transported to Pukou to cross the river. (3) He hoped that the students in Shanghai would follow the spirit of Peking University and fight together. After Xu's speech, Jiang Xueqian, the representative of Central University, rose and reported on the situation of the mass student movement in Beijing: (1) The mass movement has become more积极 in urging the government. (2) The general demonstration in the capital yesterday (i.e., the day before yesterday) involved 5,000 to 6,000 people and was very orderly. (3) The problems of food and lodging for Shanghai students going to Beijing can all be solved. (4) The arrested students of the Peking University delegation have been押至 to Peiping. After the two men spoke, the atmosphere in the entire venue became very tense. Then, other cases were discussed until the meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. Ambush Situation When the meeting adjourned, representatives from various universities went out one after another. All the directors went upstairs to the office to handle affairs. The two representatives from Peking University and Central University, because they were new to Shanghai, were busy exchanging greetings with the directors and representatives. It was not until all the representatives had dispersed that they also went out together. As soon as they went down the stone steps, beside the car parked in front of the steps, suddenly twenty or thirty plainclothes armed men rushed forward and violently beat the two representatives. The two representatives frantically cried for help and tried their best to resist, but they were outnumbered and dragged into the prepared car. At this time, the two men were still trying to struggle. Jiang, the representative of Central University, struggled and jumped out of the car. At this time, Wen Guangyi, Lin Zuyu, and other directors in the venue also came out after hearing the news and tried to rescue him, successfully rescuing Jiang from danger. However, Xu from Peking University was kidnapped and his whereabouts are still unknown. One of the assailants was captured on the spot, named Wang Fusheng, and escorted to the nearby police station. The rest of the assailants had already escaped.

Students' Statement According to a student from a certain school who witnessed the incident, there were more than ten plainclothes people eavesdropping in the venue at that time, acting like they were monitoring. Whenever students spoke, they loudly disturbed them, but the students still endured it and continued the meeting. Tao Baichuan, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, initially attended, but suddenly withdrew halfway. It was reported that representatives from Cultural and Tongji Universities witnessed that two of the perpetrators were cadres from a certain agency, one surnamed Liu and the other surnamed Zhang.

Post-Incident Handling At that time, representatives from various schools rushed to report to the Second District, Second Branch of the nearby Public Security Bureau. By the time the police arrived, the plainclothes people had already dispersed. Meanwhile, several representatives from a certain school hired a car to send the injured Jiang Xueqian, the representative of Central University, to Baolong Hospital on Baike Road for treatment. Representatives from various schools were extremely indignant, some even shedding tears. They then moved to Minli Middle School to continue the meeting and immediately decided on the handling of the tragedy: (1) The Public Security Bureau must immediately find the representative from Peking University. (2) Please the authorities to severely punish the perpetrators. (3) Please the Public Security Bureau to guarantee that this kind of tragedy will not happen again. (4) Punish the derelict head of the Second District, Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau. (5) Please the Public Security Bureau to bear the cost of the injured student's losses and medical expenses. According to a representative from a certain school speaking to the Huadong News Agency reporter, when the tragedy occurred, the police巡警 of the Public Security Bureau were very close by. Therefore, the Public Security Bureau bears considerable responsibility for this tragedy.

Jiang's Injuries Jiang Xueqian, the representative of Central University, was severely beaten and injured, with several wounds on his head and nose, his face covered in blood, and also injuries to his lower body. At about 1:00 PM, he was taken to Baolong Hospital on Baike Road for treatment under the name of Xu, and entered Ward 106. He was discharged from the hospital at about 5:00 PM that afternoon and secretly moved to another place for recuperation, fearing that something unexpected might happen.

Going to the Public Security Bureau After the University Association sent Jiang to Baolong Hospital, it sent several representatives to the Public Security Bureau to see Director Chen Xizeng. Director Chen personally received them. The student representatives requested four points: (1) Find out the whereabouts of the representative from Peking University. (2) Severely punish the perpetrators. (3) Guarantee that this incident will not happen again in the future. (4) Severely punish the derelict officials of the Public Security Bureau (because the branch office is directly opposite the association, and they did not provide protection during the attack). Chen replied as follows: The first point is difficult to achieve in fact, but he will issue an order to all districts under his jurisdiction to strictly arrest the perpetrators. The second point is a judicial issue and the captured perpetrators will be sent to the court for trial. The third point is also difficult to achieve, because the police officers of the Public Security Bureau are in charge of security and can only suppress incidents after they occur, and there is no possibility of preventing them before they happen. The fourth point, if the personnel of the Public Security Bureau are indeed derelict in their duties, they will be punished according to the law.

The Perpetrator Confesses The captured perpetrator, Wang Fusheng, after being captured by the students, was handed over to the police station and transferred to the General Bureau. At 5:00 PM in the afternoon, he was escorted to the District Court. Wang confessed that he was a worker at the Ordnance Factory. On this day, after eating, he went to the factory to work and was waiting there for a tram to Gaochang Temple to take the tram. Unexpectedly, before the tram arrived, a large number of university students suddenly came out from inside and passed by him. Suddenly, an incident of thugs beating people occurred, and he was arrested. He did not know anything else.

Today's Conference Since the tragedy occurred, the student community has been very indignant. It is reported that an emergency joint conference of university and middle school representatives from the city will be convened at 9:00 AM this morning to decide on measures to address this tragedy.

Petition to the Municipal Government After this incident occurred yesterday, more than 500 students from Jiao Tong University first went to the Municipal Government to petition at 3:30 PM in the afternoon. Soon, students from Guanghua, Daxia, Fazheng, Fudan, Liangjiang, Art Academy, Jiangnan College, Merchant Marine School, and the Chinese Students Association of Japan also arrived in droves. Students from Jinan University finally walked to the scene, totaling no less than 5,000 people. When students from Guanghua and Jiao Tong Universities first arrived at the Municipal Government, the gates of the Municipal Government were guarded by student volunteers. They first elected representatives to request an audience with Mayor Zhang and put forward four conditions: (1) No suppression of the anti-Japanese movement. (2) Release the arrested students. (3) Punish the Director of the Public Security Bureau. (4) Punish the Municipal Party personnel. When the students petitioned, Mayor Zhang happened to be meeting with Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee, so he asked Secretary-General Yu to represent him in receiving them on the Municipal Government square. However, all the students insisted that Mayor Zhang personally reply. Zhang had no choice but to personally receive all the petitioning students in the Municipal Government square at 4:15 PM. When Mayor Zhang received them, he first asked the student representatives to state the incident. The representative of Jiao Tong University then stated to Mayor Zhang, roughly saying that when the universities held a joint conference this morning, there were many plainclothes armed personnel stationed in the venue. When the meeting adjourned, these plainclothes personnel suddenly took out guns and kidnapped Jiang Xueqian, the student representative of Central University, and Xu Xiucen, the student representative of Peking University. When intercepting the representative of Central University at that time, the students on the scene personally saw Zhang, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, holding his hand tightly. Fortunately, Jiang managed to break free with all his strength, but he was already seriously injured and is now sick in Baolong Hospital. As for Xu Xiucen, the student representative of Peking University, he was kidnapped and his life and death are still unknown. What is most suspicious is that the Second District, Second Branch office is very close by, but it has never asked about this matter, so it is believed that this incident is organized and the Public Security Bureau cannot shirk its responsibility. The students had petitioned the Public Security Bureau earlier, but Director Chen's reply was not satisfactory, so they are asking to see the Mayor and requesting a satisfactory reply, and please accept all the terms and immediately release the arrested students. After Mayor Zhang listened to the student representatives' statement of the situation, he immediately replied to each condition: (1) Since the Northeast Incident occurred, it has been eighty days, and the Municipal Government has never suppressed the national salvation movement. (2) Release the arrested students. At this moment, there is no confirmation whether the students have been arrested, but he will decide with his conscience and investigate tonight, and tomorrow (i.e., today) he will ask the schools to send representatives to give a detailed reply. (3) Punish the responsible personnel, and will definitely investigate and deal with them. (4) The Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government are parallel agencies, and the Municipal Government has no authority to deal with them, but it can send a letter to inquire about everything. When Zhang replied, he asked all the students to return to school as soon as possible, and he would be responsible for everything and handle it properly. At that time, after all the students listened to Zhang's reply, some students expressed dissatisfaction and expressed their opinions on the spot, urging Zhang to immediately release Xu Xiucen, otherwise all the students vowed not to return to school. Zhang said that it was difficult to do so immediately in terms of procedures, and asked all the students to forgive him. At that time, some students shouted and asked Mayor Zhang to order the Public Security Bureau to release them by phone. Zhang had no choice but to agree to call the Public Security Bureau to inquire about everything. It was already 7:00 PM, and the large group of students waited quietly on the Municipal Government Square and the side of the Municipal Government Road, listening quietly for news. However, when Zhang called the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the sound of the phone calls back and forth was糢糊, and the whole situation was still not clear. He sent Secretary-General Yu to the Public Security Bureau to investigate. When Yu set off, he first explained the reason to all the students before getting into the car and leaving.

Representatives Meeting At this time, students from various schools arrived one after another, so they urgently convened an emergency meeting of representatives, and publicly elected Zheng Jie of Daxia University as chairman and Wang Yaodong of Fazheng as secretary, and decided that the common demands had three purposes: (1) Release the arrested students. (2) Execute the Director of the Public Security Bureau. (3) Execute the perpetrators and instigators.

Zhang Qun's Reply Mayor Zhang met with the students repeatedly after 8:00 PM and earnestly replied to the students' requests. As of this newspaper's press time, a total of seven points had been answered: (1) I will not leave the Municipal Government until I meet with the students arrested at Peking University. (2) The perpetrators will be handed over to the public, but the government must be asked for instructions and be responsible for requesting the government to execute them. (3) Regarding the Director of the Public Security Bureau, an edict will be issued immediately to suspend him from his duties pending investigation. (4) Be responsible for negotiating with the court and immediately hand over the perpetrators. (5) No suppression of the mass movement. (6) The instigator will be handled together with the second item. (7) Immediately issue an order to arrest and apprehend Tao Baichuan. Students Did Not Disperse At about 10:00 PM, Secretary-General Yu returned to the government and reported that the perpetrators had been transferred to the District Court for punishment according to law. The students insisted that the perpetrators must be brought to the Municipal Government and tried in public, and demanded that they would not disperse until the arrested Peking University students were released and met. After Mayor Zhang's earnest persuasion was ineffective, Police Commander Xiong Shihui also sent two aides to the Municipal Government at about 11:00 PM to address the crowd on behalf of Xiong, urging them to go back and rest for the time being, and to wait for Commander Xiong and Mayor Zhang to discuss a solution at length, which would definitely satisfy everyone. However, they were also rejected by the students. As of 3:00 AM this morning, all the students were still standing erect in the square in front of the Municipal Government and did not disperse.

Chen's Suspension Order Mayor Zhang issued an order last night to suspend Chen Xizeng, Director of the Public Security Bureau, for investigation. The original order stated: "This afternoon, when students from various universities held a meeting, there were situations in which students were beaten and injured by thugs and kidnapped. The Director of the Bureau was negligent in prevention beforehand and even more unable to solve the case quickly afterward, which is a dereliction of duty. His crime is inexcusable. He is hereby suspended from his duties pending investigation." This order is addressed to Chen Xizeng, Director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, Zhang Qun, December 9. It is reported that Chen will not go to the bureau to work starting today, and his duties will be performed by Chief Inspector Wang on his behalf.

Arrest Tao Baichuan Mayor Zhang issued an order last night to investigate and arrest Tao Baichuan. According to reports from students from Jiao Tong, Guanghua, Fudan, and Daxia Universities, when students from various universities held a meeting this afternoon, there were situations in which students were beaten and injured and kidnapped, and it was claimed that Tao Baichuan was the instigator, and it was requested that he be arrested and punished according to law. Based on this, it is appropriate to order the Public Security Bureau to quickly investigate and arrest Tao Baichuan, bring him to justice for investigation and handling. This order, Zhang Qun, December 9.

Party Headquarters Destroyed Yesterday afternoon at 5:50 PM, about 300 students organized a team to petition the Municipal Party Headquarters, taking four Ningbo搬場 cars and two Chinese搬場 cars. When they arrived, because no one was responsible for receiving them, it aroused public anger and they vandalized the objects in the department's Civil Training Section reception room and office. At that time, Standing Committee Member Tao Baichuan was still in the office and left shortly thereafter. Afterwards, the Municipal Party Headquarters issued a notice saying: "To whom it may concern, at about 6:00 PM this afternoon, reactionary elements incited a group of students to suddenly come to the Municipal Party Headquarters to carry out harassment and destroy all equipment. The reasons and details of what happened will be notified in another article. Fearing that the rumors are untrue, we will first send a letter. Sincerely, Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters, December 9." French Concession Martial Law The French Concession's 捕心 suddenly announced martial law at about 7:00 PM. All the iron gates at the border between the Chinese and French concessions were closed, and all the trams only drove to Xiaobeimen and no longer entered the Chinese concession. Armed police were added to patrol the streets, and the situation was serious.

京粤代表今日可聚首 92

The representatives of Beijing and Guangdong are expected to meet today

胡漢民留港養疴

Hu Hanmin Remains in Hong Kong to Recuperate

孫科等今午抵滬

Sun Ke and Others Arrive in Shanghai This Afternoon

京代表留滬候晤

Beijing Representatives Remain in Shanghai to Await Meeting

Following the selection of members from both the Beijing and Guangdong factions for the first plenary session of the Fourth Central Executive and Supervisory Committees, the Guangdong faction specially dispatched Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, and others to Shanghai to negotiate. The President Coolidge, the ship on which Sun and his party were traveling, is expected to arrive in port this afternoon. Representatives from the Guangdong faction, including Chen Mingshu and Li Shizeng, are also temporarily staying in Shanghai to meet with Sun and his party and discuss all matters. Hu Hanmin sent a telegram from Hong Kong yesterday stating that due to increased blood pressure, he would remain in Hong Kong to rest and would be unable to come to Shanghai. The information obtained yesterday is recorded below:

孫等今午到滬

Sun Ke and Others Arrive in Shanghai This Afternoon

After the conclusion of the Fourth Plenary Session of Guangdong, four representatives, Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, Chen Youren, and Li Wenfan, along with secretaries Liang Hancao, Chen Jianru, and others, traveled from Hong Kong on the President Coolidge of the Shanghai Tug and Lighter Company two days ago, and are expected to arrive here at 12:30 this afternoon. The company has specially prepared a small tugboat to depart from the Bund Customs Pier on Sanma Road at 12:30 to head to Pudong to pick up passengers. The representatives, including Sun Ke, will then take the tugboat across the river and disembark at the Customs Pier.

胡氏電告留港

Hu Hanmin Telegraphed to Stay in Hong Kong

Mr. Hu's residence in Shanghai received a telegram from Mr. Hu in Hong Kong last night stating that his blood pressure had increased to more than 18 degrees higher than when he was in Shanghai, so he could not travel with Sun Ke and Wang Jingwei. He plans to stay in Hong Kong for a period of rest. It is said that Hu's blood pressure was around 156 degrees when he was in Shanghai, and after arriving in Guangdong, it gradually increased to over 170 degrees.

陳李等特留滬

Chen Mingshu, Li Shizeng and Others Remain in Shanghai

Regarding the convening of the first plenary session of the Fourth Central Committee, the Beijing faction plans to convene it in Nanjing in mid-month. Beijing representatives Cai Yuanpei and others have previously asked Wang Jingwei to telegraph the Guangdong faction to urge them to elect members of the Central Committee to go south. Now that Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, and others have been dispatched to Shanghai and are expected to arrive this afternoon, Chen Mingshu, Li Shizeng and others have decided to remain in Shanghai temporarily to meet with Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, Chen Youren, Li Wenfan, Wang Jingwei, Zou Lu, and others to discuss all matters. As for the convening of the meeting, it is rumored that there are no major problems, and significant progress will be made after Sun Ke, Wang Jingwei and others meet first.

靑年援馬團昨日已抵南翔 93

Youth Support-Ma Expedition Arrived in Nanxiang Yesterday

萬人揮淚送征人

Ten Thousand People Tearfully Bid Farewell to the Expeditionaries

The Youth Volunteer Corps to Support General Ma and Resist Japan in Northeast China, originally scheduled to depart from Zhenru this morning, was moved by the news in the newspapers yesterday morning of General Ma Xiufang's telegram to the corps. They immediately mobilized and departed yesterday morning. The corps leader, Zhang Shaojie, came to Shanghai to send a telegram to Chairman Ma. The situation is recorded below:

團員出發

Expedition Members Depart

Yesterday morning, after members of the corps discovered General Ma Zhanshan's telegram requesting assistance for the youth in Heilongjiang in the newspapers, they immediately convened an emergency meeting. After a unanimous decision, many said they would commit suicide if they could not go to Heilongjiang immediately. Therefore, they decided to depart immediately regardless of everything and sent Zhang Shaojie to Shanghai to send a telegram to General Ma Zhanshan. The personal belongings originally carried by each person were abandoned, and instead, two people shared one set of luggage for easy carrying.

各界送别

People from All Walks of Life Bid Farewell

Upon hearing that the corps was departing, no fewer than ten thousand people came to bid farewell. Everyone shed tears. When the faculty and students of Jinan University were about to part, they donated over 300 yuan. Many students even boycotted classes to send the corps to Nanxiang. The villagers who came to see them off also tearfully presented them with copper coins and food.

路局備車

Railway Bureau Prepares Cars

Zhenru Station had prepared a special first-class car for the corps to go to Beijing. The railway staff also contacted the corps, but the corps politely declined. When they were about to leave, the railway police saluted them.

加入團員

New Members Join the Expedition

Chen JiongHao, a nurse from the Wusong Sanatorium, Li Kezhai, an overseas Chinese from Siam, and others walked from Shanghai to Jinan University the night before to gather and depart. Yesterday morning, several members of the Indian Alliance Association rushed to Zhenru, expressing their willingness to cooperate with the corps and go north together. However, due to language barriers and nationality issues, it was difficult to travel together. The corps politely expressed their sincere acceptance of their kindness, but due to various practical issues, they could not easily agree. The Indians expressed their disappointment with understanding. The corps also received a letter from Mr. Xu Fuyuan of Suzhou yesterday, which roughly stated: The loyal and unparalleled General Ma has been defeated again. Fuyuan's heart is about to break. I regret that I cannot fly to the Northeast to fight those Japanese bandits. Fortunately, you comrades have formed a corps to support Ma in Heilongjiang. The bravery and grand style are what a real man should do in this world. I am willing to join you enthusiastically and share life and death with you comrades, sprinkling my blood on the black walls to fulfill my original intention. I sincerely hope you will not refuse. If you cannot agree, I will end my life. It is said that Mr. Xu is waiting at the Suzhou station to join the corps.

團長來滬

Corps Leader Comes to Shanghai

After the corps departed on foot, they sent the corps leader, Zhang Shaojie, to Shanghai to send a telegram. Chen Zhenru and He Jingzhi were trying to invite the corps leader to talk. Mr. Zhang then went to Mr. Chen's residence on Ga'en Road to meet him. It is said that the two gentlemen offered encouragement and Mr. Chen made some gifts.

粤方代表

Guangdong Representatives

Wang Jingwei and Zou Haibin heard that Mr. Zhang had come to Shanghai and immediately invited him to talk. However, due to time constraints, Mr. Zhang was unable to meet with them. Zou Haibin relayed the opinions of Wang and Zou, hoping that the members of the corps would cherish their bodies and not lightly sacrifice their lives, and hoped that they would be wary of Japanese spies along the way.

致海倫電

Telegram to Hailun

Hailun 转马主席占山钧鉴，齐电奉悉，吾公独抗倭奴，敬仰无涯，中华民族之一线生机，端赖吾公之最后奋斗，慨自倭奴逞暴以来，全国军人，袖手旁观，各党各派，争权夺利，民族之危亡，同胞之惨痛，不堪言状，我公既能独抗，我等何忍偷生，明知力微势薄，天寒路远，然覆巢之下，必无完卵，与其死于贼手，不若死于杀贼，即或不能到达东北，亦愿以我等热血与灵魂，唤醒中华民族，为我五千年历史争光荣，使世界知中华民族尚未死绝，使吾辈青年，知世间尚有继续牺牲之份子，倘继起有人，虽死何恨，年来党派纷歧，亡国之象已具，与其做内战之工具，曷若为民族生存而流血，我等现已下必死决心，誓与吾公同生死，与东北共存亡，请吾公保重，奋斗到底，勿以为念，我等均属强壮青年，热血沸腾，决心不惜一切，现已兼程离沪，沿途组合，苟吾全国同胞，一致自动前往，区区倭奴，何足道哉，临电感泣，不知所云，

To Chairman Ma Zhanshan of Hailun: We have received your telegram. We deeply admire your heroic resistance against the Japanese invaders. The last hope of the Chinese nation depends on your final struggle. Since the Japanese invaders began their violence, the national army has stood by idly, and various parties and factions have been fighting for power and profit. The peril of the nation and the suffering of our compatriots are indescribable. Since you are able to resist alone, how can we bear to live in ease? We know that our strength is weak, the weather is cold, and the journey is long, but when the nest is overturned, no egg remains intact. Rather than dying at the hands of the enemy, it is better to die killing the enemy. Even if we cannot reach the Northeast, we are willing to use our blood and souls to awaken the Chinese nation, to win glory for our 5,000-year history, to let the world know that the Chinese nation is not dead, and to let us young people know that there are still those who are willing to continue to sacrifice. If there are successors, we will have no regrets even if we die. In recent years, the party factions have been divided, and the signs of national subjugation are evident. Rather than being tools of internal strife, why not shed blood for the survival of the nation? We have now made a resolution to die, vowing to live and die with you and to coexist with the Northeast. Please take care of yourself and fight to the end. Do not worry about us. We are all strong young people, full of enthusiasm, and determined to spare no effort. We are now leaving Shanghai at an accelerated pace, organizing along the way. If our compatriots across the country would go forward together voluntarily, how could a small Japanese nation be worth mentioning? In the telegram, with tears in our eyes, we do not know what to say.

内部組織

Internal Organization

The internal organization of the corps is divided into three levels: ordinary members, selected outstanding members as basic members, and further selected outstanding members as cadres. Special attention is paid to the training of all members' thoughts and actions. A military library has been established, and more than 20 books on China-Japan and Northeast China events have been purchased, and donations are being solicited from various bookstores. The corps' only major goal is to offer no resistance internally, but to kill the enemy and achieve results externally.

隨軍記乾

Military Correspondents

Chen Chongwei (i.e., Chen Chongsheng), the author of "The Westward Journey of Yan Yi Ji," and Gan Jingtang are traveling with the corps as military correspondents.

南翔歡迎

Welcome in Nanxiang

The corps arrived in Nanxiang at noon yesterday. The local party headquarters and business and academic circles held a welcome meeting at the Guqi Garden. They were both joyful and indignant at the meeting, and ended up shedding tears while speaking. The corps decided to stay in Nanxiang that day and proceed to Kunshan this morning.

临别赠言

Parting Words

Huang Jingwan and others from the National Endeavor Society gave parting words at the farewell, which roughly included: (1) Do not forget the expectations of the people in the rear; (2) Pay attention to military hygiene; (3) Arouse the people everywhere and organize support associations; (4) The majority should take care of the minority; (5) Understand the special difficulties of female comrades; (6) Report the situation to the rear at any time, etc. The corps has expressed its acceptance of each item.

組後援會

Organizing Support Associations

The Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff in Shanghai, the Shanghai Volunteer Army, the National Endeavor Society, and others held a special meeting yesterday to organize a support association for the corps, arouse the people, continue the spirit of the corps, and appointed Sun Mujia, Huang Jingwan, Wang Longzhou, and others to draft the charter. It is also said that the rear advisors of the corps will hold a meeting today to discuss the matter.

南洋募捐

Donations in Southeast Asia

The rear communications of the corps are being handled by advisors such as Pan Xulun in Shanghai, and the Shanghai Bank is collecting donations. In Southeast Asia, the Hefeng Bank is collecting donations to be responsible for the corps' Southeast Asian donation team. The solicitors are Chen Fen and Chen Shusun (both from Guangdong) from the China Public School, Chen Shihao from Fudan University, and Liang Ziqiang (overseas Chinese) from Jinan University. They will leave Shanghai tomorrow morning on the Taikoo Company's Qingyuan Wheel. After arriving in Hong Kong, they will depart to solicit donations and recruit members to go north on the various islands of Southeast Asia for about ten days. Then, they will go to Guangzhou to raise funds and then take a ship back to Shanghai with the members recruited along the way, and then go north to join the corps to resist Japan and support Ma.

又有援馬鉅欵滙哈 94

Another Large Amount of Money is Remitted to Harbin for Supporting Ma

電政同人匯一千元

Telecom Personnel Remit 1,000 Yuan

After Nie Chuanru, Huang Zhicheng, Guo Shihuan, Gu Guangbin and more than ten other section chiefs from the Department of Telecom Administration of the Ministry of Communications initiated the assistance to Chairman Ma of Heilongjiang Province, donations from various places have been very enthusiastic. All funds are entrusted to the Telecom Public Welfare Association for remittance. As of yesterday, more than 1,500 yuan had been received. In addition, there is still a considerable amount of money that has been remitted but has not arrived. The association has already telegraphed 1,000 yuan in advance yesterday. The telegram from the association to Chairman Ma is recorded below. "To Chairman Ma of Hailun: Your lone army resists Japan and uniquely expresses your public loyalty. Your fame has spread, and the whole country admires you. Telecom personnel are willing to collect resources and provide support. We will first telegraph 1,000 yuan from the Bank of China to help with military expenses. We will continue to remit more when we have accumulated sufficient funds. We hereby send this telegram and await good news. The China National Telecom Personnel Public Welfare Association, respectfully."

廣肇員生匯一千元

Staff and Students of Guangzhao Public School Remit 1,000 Yuan

The staff and students of Guangzhao Public School telegraphed Ma Zhanshan and all the officers and soldiers, saying, "The fall of Liaoning and Jilin has aroused indignation throughout the country. Our generals and soldiers are uniquely able to repeatedly defeat the powerful and enhance the glory of the nation. We are remitting 1,000 yuan in silver dollars to the Citibank of Harbin to express our admiration. Please receive and reply, and we hope that you will continue to strive to kill the enemy and restore our territory. Thank you very much." Ma Zhanshan replied in a telegram, "To the staff and students of Guangzhao Public School in Shanghai: I have received your telegram. Thank you for your praise and generous donation. On behalf of my comrades-in-arms, I extend my remote thanks. The provincial government has now moved to Hailun County in eastern China. Your donation has been assigned to be transferred to Harbin. Sincerely, Ma Zhanshan."

抗日會設計會議紀 96

Minutes of the Design Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association

通過扣貨標準草案

Draft Standards for Seizing Goods Passed

The Design Committee of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held its eighth committee meeting at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce the other day. More than ten members attended, including Deng Zenao, Jin Runxiang, Li Wenjie, Pan Xulun, Zhu Wenqi, and Xie Zhongfu. Zhu Wenqi was elected chairman to discuss the following important cases: (1) Deng Zenao, Lu Fengzhu, Lu Qisheng, and other three committee members proposed a draft of the standards for seizing goods, which has now been completed. They requested a public decision. The decision was made that the five items of the standards for seizing goods be approved as originally proposed, and that Li Wenjie, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Qisheng, and other three committee members review and supplement the inspection and seizure procedures in accordance with the previous resolutions. (2) The Standing Committee submitted a proposal for reviewing the measures to punish treacherous merchants who resist inspection of enemy goods. The decision was made that the review opinions are as follows: If a treacherous merchant illegally resists inspection, and the facts are proven, a request for punishment should be made, and the following four measures should be implemented (the measures are unchanged from the original proposal). The above two cases should be sent to the Standing Committee for reference and implementation. (3) Xue Hanguang's statement on preparing for war against Japan was passed on for review by Committee Member Xie Zhongfu. (4) The appointment of Lian Qitai, Bei Zuyi, and Jiang Wanping as design committee members was approved, and the Executive Committee was requested to send letters of appointment.

Dock Workers of Japanese Companies

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Dock Workers of Japanese Companies held its third regular meeting yesterday. The case was handed over to the secretariat to reply to the Trade Union Federation based on the findings of the investigation. (2) Workers from the Xinhui Mountain Wharf reported that recently some Japanese were buying off workers in an attempt to disrupt the work of other wharves and cause riots. The case was handed over to the investigation department in conjunction with the propaganda department to conduct a thorough investigation for verification. (3) Cao Yizhi proposed that the association should hire two clerks, and requested that Shen Haiquan and Wang Dasan be appointed. The resolution was passed. (4) Liu Xingbo proposed that there are tens of thousands of workers in various wharves, and it is inevitable that there will be both good and bad. Once they are lured by others, it is a cause for concern. The secretary should be instructed to draft a letter to the workers, explaining the general meaning of resisting Japan and saving the country. The resolution was passed to the propaganda department for extensive publicity. (5) Cao Yizhi proposed that the association has stipulated that every Monday morning is a day for expanded propaganda. All staff members in the association should cooperate with the propaganda department and go to the wharves to carry out propaganda. The resolution was passed. (6) Liu Yongyan proposed that the association should produce badges and distribute them to all staff members for identification. He now proposed a style for public decision. The resolution was passed and handed over to the general affairs department to purchase 200 pieces according to the style for distribution. The meeting adjourned.
