Youth Corner

Women Under the Three Principles of the People 179

— Mr. Ye Ranchuo's Speech at the Qingdao Women's Zhengyi Association, Notes by Ms. Chen Yunhuang

Ladies and gentlemen, I am very pleased and honored that your esteemed association has asked me to say a few words today.

However, I did not prepare beforehand, so I can only offer a few rambling remarks as a contribution. Since arriving in Qingdao, the thing that has made me happiest is the social work that your esteemed association is doing. To be able to work so enthusiastically in such a quiet atmosphere is worthy of attention. Today, I will use "Women Under the Three Principles of the People" as my topic for discussion. Why do we want to discuss this topic? Everyone knows that the National Government was founded on the Three Principles of the People and is governed by them.

These two sentences have been heard and seen so many times on various propaganda materials and slogans posted on walls that everyone is tired of them. Because they are seen too often and are too common, these propaganda and slogans fail to arouse stimulation and attention. However, upon careful study, they are of great value and have a profound relationship with the future of the country. So, how should women under the Three Principles of the People act? This is worthy of our discussion. According to a recent postal survey, the Chinese population is nearly 500 million, of which women account for 250 million. Ladies and gentlemen, you must understand that the strength of a modern country depends entirely on whether all the citizens can unite, not on the talents of one or two heroes. In the past, relying on a few leaders to command the army could defeat the enemy. Now, with the progress of public opinion, national responsibility rests on the shoulders of the general public. We often hear the slogan "Total National Mobilization," which means that every citizen should bear responsibility. To take the smallest example, during the European War, the people of the belligerent countries saved their own bread and transported it to the front to feed the soldiers. This is the meaning of total national mobilization.

Our country is an industrially backward country. Our various industries are far behind others, causing the people of the whole country to suffer all kinds of oppression. If we want the country to survive, we will be powerless without total national mobilization. In the past, when we talked about patriotism, we were just talking about it. We never really felt the pain deeply. In the last ten years, various trends have surged and impacted. The world's major powers have also been greatly affected by economic oppression, let alone China, with its underdeveloped industry and unorganized politics. In this situation,

coupled with the continuous succession of natural disasters over the years, the floods you just mentioned are only one of them. People say that China has a vast territory and abundant resources, but in fact, China has a vast territory but not abundant resources. Let's take our daily necessities as an example. Our country is based on agriculture, and the people's food and clothing should have been very abundant, but now the silk and cotton we use are mostly imported. Rice is also imported from Japan, Annam, and Siam. Flour is imported from Canada. Even the materials for the houses we live in and the roads we walk on have to rely on foreigners. In short, it can be said that the clothes we wear are given to us by others, the food we eat is given to us by others, the houses we live in are given to us by others, and the roads we walk on are given to us by others. In other words, we have to rely on others to have clothes to wear, food to eat, houses to live in, and roads to walk on. Food, clothing, housing, and transportation are the four essential elements of people's daily life. If we rely on others, not only will the losses be too great, but the danger will be very great.

According to recent reports from disaster relief workers, at least 200,000 to 300,000 people have died in the floods in our country this time. In the past ten years or so, a total of about one million people have died in various places due to natural and man-made disasters, but the people of the country have not awakened, and the civil war continues unabated. China has reached a time of great calamity. Therefore, I say that if China is to survive, everyone must work together. Men should work hard, and women should also fulfill their national responsibilities. We should make special efforts regarding unexpected things. Just like the European War mentioned above, the people of the belligerent countries saved bread and supplied it to the soldiers. This is a method of saving the country by the people. The power of the people is great and deep, and its efficiency surpasses the great achievements of heroes who succeed by chance. If the people have shallow knowledge and cannot unite, even if one or two heroes fight for the country, they will be powerless. If the people of the whole country can fulfill their respective responsibilities, then their country will be strong. Therefore, we should not have the mindset of "not doing anything unless it is a big deal," and we should not fail to fulfill our responsibilities to the country unless we are in high positions. Every man and every woman in China should quickly

Page 18

awaken, unite spontaneously, and work together.

Now, let's talk briefly about the Three Principles of the People. Let's start with nationalism. Is the Chinese nation healthy? Is its solidarity strong? Let us examine the reasons why it is not healthy and not strong. Where is the root cause? Since the success of the revolution, the five ethnic groups are in a republic, meaning that the five ethnic groups should be equal. But are the knowledge levels of the five ethnic groups equal? Are the knowledge and abilities of the 500 million people healthy? It is difficult to improve the nation now, but the most important part is to improve the knowledge and abilities of the 250 million women. Women account for half of the entire Chinese nation. If this half of the women can bear considerable responsibility for the country, their power will definitely be great. The greatest difficulty for women is the physical disadvantage. If we want the entire nation to be healthy, we must first ensure that the physical strength of half of the women is healthy. Therefore, eugenics in recent times is not just empty talk and is very worthy of study.

Secondly, let's talk about the principle of democracy. The Premier divided power into two things: authority and ability. However, the two must be connected. Those with authority must have "ability." Those without ability should not have authority. Nowadays, people only know how to fight for power, but they do not talk about ability. If abilities are not cultivated well and one obtains power, not only may it not be used well, but it may even harm the country. I hope women will understand the current situation of China and their own position and should strive to seek "ability." In the future constitutional period, they will certainly be able to achieve the goal of participating in politics and holding political power.

Finally, let's talk about the principle of people's livelihood. China has reached a time of poverty and exhaustion. At this time, it is impossible to escape the economic oppression of other countries. Most wealthy people are extravagant and use aristocratic Western goods exclusively. The poor also love to look good and rush to buy cheap Eastern goods. The people's livelihood of the country is almost completely plundered by foreigners. Therefore, it can be said that it is difficult for China to escape its status as a semi-colony. Is this because China has no fundamental solution, or is it because the people are not awakened and do not work hard? I think our China is not a country that has no fundamental solution. For daily necessities, we should use domestic products as much as possible and strive to improve and increase production capacity. Nowadays, people in our country compete to look good and do not care about practicality. This is true not only for the rich in cities, but also for the peasants in remote rural areas. Therefore, they reject domestic products and rush to use foreign goods, causing the national interest to be taken away by foreigners without any regard. If our 500 million compatriots make up their minds that ordinary daily necessities must be domestic products, then when the supply falls short of demand, the people of the country will definitely rise up to find ways to increase production. As for the equipment and machinery needed in education, science, industry, and military affairs, we can temporarily purchase foreign goods. This requires the government to cultivate specialized talents. After ten years, it can be successful. Our Republic of China has the materials for development and the land for development, but it is because the people of the whole country do not have the determination to develop that the country's livelihood is becoming increasingly poor. It is a pity. I remember that during the European War, Japan lacked food and hoped that the United States would lend him 350,000 tons of rice every year. The relationship between the United States and Japan has always been bad, so they were unwilling to agree. Later, Japan repeatedly requested, and the United States only allowed him to exchange it for 350,000 tons of ships. The Japanese authorities had to sacrifice in order to take care of the people's food, but after being stimulated by this, they worked extremely hard. Now, Japanese rice is being transported to our country. The Chinese nation, which claims to be based on agriculture, relies on foreigners for much of its food and clothing, which is not only shameful, but has reached a terrible time. Regarding clothing, you women should pay more attention.

In recent years, almost all of the materials for women's clothing have been imported. Our country originally had very good silk, satin, damask, and gauze, but because the patterns were slightly inferior, most women were unwilling to wear them, so things like georgette and Indian silk greatly catered to the psychology of women. Although they are thin and expensive, they do not care. In addition, the leather shoes and silk stockings on the feet, the shirts and undershirts on the body, the watches and rings on the hands, and the perfume and cosmetics on the head are all imported and are all expensive things. A leather suitcase in hand can be worth dozens of yuan. Since the price of gold has soared, the Chinese people do not know how much they have suffered. Look at the development of Japan in recent years, especially its aggression against our country, which is very alarming. Japan is an island country with a very small area. Its own country is not enough for development, so it has no choice but to invade other countries. However, it is difficult to invade other countries. If the invaded people make strong and effective resistance, Japan's development will definitely be greatly hindered. Under such difficulties, Japan's development has shocked the world. As the saying goes, "It depends on people." The people of China should wake up. As mentioned above, China has a vast territory but not abundant resources, but with this vast land, it is easy to develop. The way to develop does not have to be to invade other countries. Just work hard in your own home, and you can compete with the richest country in the world, the United States. Not only will the people's livelihood be free of problems from then on, but also it can supply the needs of people in other countries. Now, all countries in the world have special developments, but China not only has no development in anything, but also relies on others for everything, resulting in a crisis. I think it is not that China has no fundamental solution, but that a small number of leaders in China are not up to par, which makes the majority of the people follow suit. As a result, everyone complains about heaven and blames others, pointing fingers at each other. Having reached this point, it is absolutely inappropriate to be so bored. Everyone should cheer up and work hard. It is useless to just complain about each other. Half of my fellow female compatriots should not give up their responsibilities. For example, if we plant a tree and never see it grow up and expect it to wither day by day, we should study the reasons. Is it because the land is not good, or is someone ruining it? I can say that the land in China is considered very fertile and very suitable for planting in the world, so it is not that the land is not good. It is indeed the people themselves who are ruining it. One person ruins it in this way, and everyone else does not have the responsibility to protect it, and even ruins it casually. If everyone is willing to make up their minds to protect it, it will definitely grow very luxuriantly. Half of my fellow female compatriots should bear the responsibility of joint protection and joint cultivation. But we must understand the phenomena of Chinese society, carefully study various cultivation methods, do not shout wildly, rush recklessly, see the objects clearly, and proceed step by step. For example, in the matter of raising money for disaster relief, everyone feels exhausted from running around. In fact, just the opium tax in Hankou alone can generate 160 million yuan a year, and cigars generate 30 million yuan a year. This is just for domestic products. I don't know how much more there is for imported goods. If our smoking compatriots all smoke one less cigarette, wouldn't that be enough to save the disaster victims of the whole country? To take it a step further, before this flood occurred, it was clear that the dikes in the Yangtze River basin were not strong, but no one was willing to do preventive work. Therefore, this flood was not an accidental natural disaster. If it does not come this year, it will come next year or the year after. Therefore, I say that China does not have a fundamental solution, but everyone has given up on themselves. Because everyone does not pay attention to everything, the country suffers.

The Chinese people have not yet eliminated family relationships. The common life in the family cannot be abolished. If women have received considerable education and are engaged in occupations, they can at least reduce part of the burden on men. When women have occupations, there can be more production and less consumption in the family. If every woman in the country reduces consumption by one yuan, then the whole country can reduce consumption by 250 million yuan. To take it a step further, if every woman in the country produces one yuan, then the country's production volume will also increase by 250 million yuan. Therefore, women have such a great relationship with national production, so women's education should also be given special attention. I often hear about overthrowing the education of virtuous wives and good mothers, which is also wrong. Virtuous wives and good mothers are not humiliating women's education. Women's education is certainly not limited to virtuous wives and good mothers. On the other hand, men are not limited to being virtuous husbands and good fathers. However, we should cooperate with each other according to our respective natures, with the goal of benefiting the country. For example, a factory is divided into a machine room and an office. You cannot say that the machine room is the factory and the office is not the factory, nor can you say that the office is important and the machine room is not important. Cooperation is necessary.

Now, China's national situation is as dangerous as a pile of eggs. Women should cooperate with men, men should not despise women, and women should not give up on themselves. As for the methods of cooperation, of course, I cannot explain them in detail here, but do not have ambition first. When you come out, you will not do anything unless it is a big deal, to show your ability and gain false reputation. You must know that even if it is a very small thing, as long as it is beneficial, you have to start. Although the matter is small, the strength of the people across the country is not small. When all men and women in the country understand this principle, they can develop internally and resist externally.

Page 19

Book Review

Japan's Past and Future Aggression Against China by Mori Chi 180

Originally written by Tenta Shukei

Published by Guanghua Bookstore

Since the occurrence of the Eastern Province Incident, nearly three months have passed in an instant. Even those who have no common sense of international politics understand that this incident is entirely a planned, step-by-step, and prepared action by Japan. No one will doubt that it is simply a "rash action by a small number of Japanese soldiers."

Some say that Japan's blatant actions this time were based on the ideas of Tanaka Giichi, while others say that they followed the policies of Yamada Takeji. In fact, the person who first initiated the plan and led the invasion of China was the famous former Minister of Finance, Tenta Shukei. The plans of Tanaka and others after that were all based on his old tricks.

Amidst the extremely high tide of anti-Japanese sentiment, I would like to introduce Tenta's book "Japan's Past and Future Aggression Against China" to the people of the country.

The contents of this book are as follows:

Chapter 1: Introduction. In the review of the necessity of invading China, he said, "The fact that such a neighboring country is now weak and declining is a great opportunity for the development of the Yamato nation. We should study and deal with it in order to soar in the continent and renew the face of the Asian race. This is truly what we should plan." Just from these few sentences, we can see that Japan's ambition to annex China is clearly evident. He also said, "China is rich in iron ore and lime, has promising oil resources, can cultivate cotton, can raise sheep, and has other materials. All the necessities for our national economy... can be obtained from China. Because of this relationship, it is most urgent to grasp the power to control China's economy from the perspective of imperial independence. I regard the China issue as the most important thing because of this. Furthermore, when we look at China's politics, there are those who advocate partition based on the power relations of various countries... However, today's consensus in the empire is that China must not be partitioned. This is not because it is in China's interest that it cannot be partitioned, but because it is in the empire's interest that it cannot be partitioned... It is better to let China nominally possess sovereignty, while the empire reaps the actual benefits." These few words have now realized his legacy. For example, the League of Nations proposed to establish a central zone in Jinzhou, but Japan openly opposed it, because it completely regards China as "a gift from heaven to the Yamato nation" and is extremely unwilling to have a third party interfere. Therefore, after the incident occurred, it absolutely advocated direct negotiations and did not propose the idea of partition. This is entirely in accordance with Tenta's will. Therefore, tracing back to the cause of this incident, Japan has used threatening means everywhere, in order to make us completely submit to him. His vicious policy is to make China nominally possess sovereignty, while Japan reaps the actual benefits, in other words, to let Japan manipulate China's economic power without incurring the crime of destroying China. Therefore, Tenta's book is nothing less than a confession of Japan's vicious policy of invading China.

Chapter 2: Sino-Japanese Friendship and Various Facilities. This chapter talks about how Japan must pretend to be friendly with China, while secretly devising ways to gradually swallow China. His heart is big, and his plan is also cunning. He said, "The Empire hopes to develop in China, so it hopes to be friendly with China." This is truly a confession of his inner heart. He also said, "However, in the past, the development in China was too eager for profit. For example, when investing in China, we hoped for too much from them, and we gained too much, which often led to disputes... It only aroused the suspicion of the Chinese people. I especially try to avoid these malpractices and follow the motto of 'giving before taking' in order to reap great benefits in the future." From this, we can know that his poisonous plan is to first give us a small profit, and then implement his economic aggression, sucking our blood, wanting to make China a blood-deficient and weak body, and forever provide it with flesh.

However, designing to invade our country certainly requires preparation and facilities. Tenta also deeply felt this necessity, so he said, "We have proposed many facilities for China, and most of them have not yet been implemented." From this, we can see that Tenta is truly the first person to mastermind the invasion of China, because many facilities were also proposed by him. At that time, the important facilities he proposed for development in China included "the improvement and reform of financial institutions in China," "loans to China," "the establishment of political affairs officials stationed in China," "the problem of financial advisors in China," "the problem of Chinese tariffs," etc. In particular, he spared no effort for the plan of Manchuria and Mongolia.

Chapter 3: The Improvement and Reform of China's Financial Institutions. Tenta was a former important figure in the Japanese Ministry of Finance. Since the Russo-Japanese War, all of Japan's economic aggression against China has involved his participation, because he has more experience in economics, especially with regard to the financial situation of China. This chapter is divided into several sections, such as the improvement and reform of financial institutions and lending institutions in Manchuria and Mongolia, the improvement and reform of financial institutions in mainland China, and details the tasks of Japanese financial institutions that invaded China, such as the Yokohama Specie Bank, the Bank of Korea, the Bank of Taiwan, the Japanese Industrial Bank, and the China and South Sea Bank. The analysis is exceptionally clear. It is clearly indicated which bank should be active in the world, which bank should be active exclusively in China, which bank should increase its reserves and set up branches in Shanghai, and which bank should manipulate the finances of Manchuria. Therefore, Tenta is a great planner for Japan and a great enemy to our country. As for mentioning the Japanese investment institutions that invaded China, his conspiracy is even more obvious. He said, "Investing in China is extremely valuable for secrecy and speed. If it is leaked before it is completed, it will not be possible to establish it even if it is of great benefit to Japan. This is what I have experienced many times. Therefore, it is most necessary to conduct it quickly and secretly under the consolidation group of these special banks." Therefore, the Oriental Development Company, the East Asia Industrial Company, and the China-Japan Industrial Company, etc., were successively established, and they invested in our country en masse to achieve their ambitions of aggression. Their investments in China are mostly biased towards railways, because they can not only profit from it, but also use the convenience of transportation to invade the interior of China. From then on, Japanese goods flooded the market like mercury poured on the ground, and Japanese colonists poured into China like carps crossing the river.

Chapter 4: An Outline of Loans to China. He said, "In order to protect the independence of Japan's national economy or national defense in the future, we cannot but occupy China... If we want to make a great country exist in East Asia, we cannot but work hard to develop China... Investing in China's economy is Japan's duty, and this matter is extremely just for China and for the world." His words are absurd and can be said to be extreme. The so-called loans to China are to lend money to the Chinese at an interest rate of 8% to establish railways and telecommunications, etc. After Japan lent money to China, on the one hand, it gained control of China's economy, and on the other hand, it gained priority in various transportation and telecommunications aspects due to the loan terms, making it an important part of aggression. He said, "The improvement of China's telecommunications... is also more convenient for our country and other countries' commercial trade, and the China and South Sea Bank can also play a role in this regard." Therefore, from this we can know that none of his conspiracies are not multi-faceted. He is truly a great conspirator that has never been seen in the world.

What Tenta could not forget the most was lending money to China to build railways, because the construction of railways could give the development of Japan's aggression the greatest benefit. Look at what he said, "When this railway is completed, the Empire will be able to connect Korea, Manchuria, and the northern provinces of China very satisfactorily... Expediting the construction of these railways is also the most important thing for the future development of Japan's mainland." What should we think?

Chapters 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9 are about the branch aspects of aggression. Some of them have become the past, and some have not yet been realized. I will not repeat them here.

In the conclusion of Chapter 10, he said, "Regarding the issue of Japan's economic superiority, I have only opened the door. As for the facilities that have been put in place to make them effectively realized, some may take several years, and some may take several decades. I hope that the government and the public will work together with one heart and one mind to ensure that this foundation is not destroyed and to work hard on this foundation to build it even more solidly." No wonder there was Tanaka's "Proactive Policy of Japan's Aggression Against Manchuria and Mongolia." From this, we can know that the September 18th Incident was also an expected event.

It is said that this book is secretly issued in Japan and distributed to important political and financial figures in the country. It was obtained by the translator after hard searching. I hope readers will read it carefully.

Book Review Guidelines 181

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all books on politics, economics, law, science, education, etc. are included in the introduction. However, vulgar books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) The pictures are limited to the latest works of new domestic and foreign artists and related illustrations.

(3) Texts on the study or investigation of ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photographs are limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each article should not exceed 3,000 words.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not draw pictures with blue ink and do not use colored paper. You must use white paper and black drawings.
